Font Awesome Pro 6.4.0 by @fontawesome - https://fontawesome.com License - https://fontawesome.com/license (Commercial License) Copyright 2023 Fonticons, Inc. --><path d=\"M47.6 300.4L228.3 469.1c7.5 7 17.4 10.9 27.7 10.9s20.2-3.9 27.7-10.9L464.4 300.4c30.4-28.3 47.6-68 47.6-109.5v-5.8c0-69.9-50.5-129.5-119.4-141C347 36.5 300.6 51.4 268 84L256 96 244 84c-32.6-32.6-79-47.5-124.6-39.9C50.5 55.6 0 115.2 0 185.1v5.8c0 41.5 17.2 81.2 47.6 109.5z\"/></svg></span> Save</a>\n                </div>\n        </div>\t\t\t\t<div class=\"byline\">\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"post_content\">\n\n<p><strong>This is hands down the best carrot cake recipe I&#8217;ve ever made.</strong> It&#8217;s easy, made from scratch, wonderfully moist in the middle, has the creamiest cream cheese frosting, and is absolutely delicious!</p>\n\n\n\n<div id=\"ytplaceholder\"><img fetchpriority=\"high\" decoding=\"async\" class=\"ytcover\" alt=\"Carrot Cake Recipe Video\" src=\"/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-Video.jpg\"><iframe id=\"ytiframe\" width=\"640\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/imJS5swk0Vc?rel=0\" title=\"YouTube video player\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe>\n</div>\n\n\n\n<p>The moment I tried this carrot cake recipe, I was hooked! The ingredient list is simple, and they come together to make such a delicious, moist, perfectly spiced cake.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I bet you already have most of what you need to make this recipe in your kitchen. This really is one of my favorite <a href=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/category/recipes/cake-recipes/\">cake recipes</a>. For cupcakes, check out our recipe for <a href=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/46269/carrot-cake-cupcakes/\" data-type=\"post\" data-id=\"46269\">carrot cake cupcakes</a>. Or for another spring inspired cake, try our <a href=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/36764/strawberry-cake-recipe/\" data-type=\"post\" data-id=\"36764\">fresh strawberry cake</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-full\"><img fetchpriority=\"high\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1800\" src=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/07/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-6-1200.jpg\" alt=\"Slice of homemade carrot cake with cream cheese frosting.\" class=\"wp-image-34936\" srcset=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/07/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-6-1200.jpg 1200w, https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/07/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-6-1200-533x800.jpg 533w, https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/07/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-6-1200-200x300.jpg 200w, https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/07/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-6-1200-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/07/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-6-1200-683x1024.jpg 683w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></figure>\n\n\n\n<h2 class=\"wp-block-heading\">Key Ingredients</h2>\n\n\n\n<ul class=\"wp-block-list\">\n<li><strong>Flour:</strong>&nbsp;I use all-purpose flour, but this recipe works with spelt flour or your favorite gluten-free flour blend for a gluten-free carrot cake.</li>\n\n\n\n<li><strong>Baking soda:</strong>&nbsp;Helps our cake rise. We don&#8217;t add baking powder (this cake recipe does not need it). Check that your baking soda has not been open for longer than 6 months (it loses its potency after that).</li>\n\n\n\n<li><strong>Sugar:</strong>&nbsp;Makes carrot cake moist and delicious. I love a combination of white and brown sugar. If you only want to use one, choose brown sugar since it has the necessary acid to react with the baking soda.</li>\n\n\n\n<li><strong>Oil:&nbsp;</strong>The secret to keeping our carrot cake so deliciously moist. I&#8217;ve used avocado oil, safflower oil, and vegetable oil with great results. Melted coconut oil works, too, but the baked cake will have a light coconut flavor.</li>\n\n\n\n<li><strong>Salt, cinnamon, and vanilla extract:</strong>&nbsp;Make our cake taste amazing, resulting in a lightly spiced cake.</li>\n\n\n\n<li><strong>Eggs:</strong>&nbsp;This cake calls for 4 eggs, which add flavor, moisture, and give the cake structure.</li>\n\n\n\n<li><strong>Carrots:</strong>&nbsp;Three cups of freshly grated carrots make this the best carrot cake! If you&#8217;re making the carrot cake and start to second-guess the number of carrots called for in our recipe, don&#8217;t. You need all three cups. It is a carrot cake, after all.</li>\n\n\n\n<li><strong>Pecans and Raisins:</strong>&nbsp;These add texture, but they are optional. Reading through the comment section, it is clear that some people love nuts and raisins in carrot cake, while others cannot stand them. I love them, but add what you love!</li>\n</ul>\n\n\n\n<h2 class=\"wp-block-heading\">How to&nbsp;Make Carrot Cake</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>If you have a couple of bowls and can stir ingredients together, you can make this easy cake! You&#8217;ll start by whisking the dry ingredients in one bowl, and do the same with the wet ingredients in another.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Making this cake batter reminds me of making <a href=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/24593/essential-pancake-recipe/\" data-type=\"post\" data-id=\"24593\">pancakes</a> or <a href=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/18982/our-favorite-easy-blueberry-muffin-recipe/\" data-type=\"post\" data-id=\"18982\">muffins</a>. All you need to do is fold the dry ingredients into the wet, add your carrots, nuts, and raisins, and you are done. It&#8217;s that easy!</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-full\"><noscript><img decoding=\"async\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\" src=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-Step_5-1200.jpg\" alt=\"Adding grated carrots to the carrot cake batter.\" class=\"wp-image-30658\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%201200%20800%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-Step_5-1200.jpg\" alt=\"Adding grated carrots to the carrot cake batter.\" class=\"lazyload wp-image-30658\" cake, divide the batter between two baking pans, and slide them into a 350\u00b0F oven. Bake the layers until they rise in the pans and are a bit bouncy when you lightly touch them. (I use one or two fingers and lightly push. If you leave a dent in the cake, it needs more time.)</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-full\"><noscript><img decoding=\"async\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\" src=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-Step_6-1200.jpg\" alt=\"baking carrot cake - pouring carrot cake batter into round cake pans before baking\" class=\"lazyload wp-image-30659\" data-srcset=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-Step_6-1200.jpg 1200w, https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-Step_6-1200-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-Step_6-1200-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-Step_6-1200-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/Carrot-Cake-Recipe-Step_6-1200-188x125.jpg 188w\" data-sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></figure>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>It&#8217;s important that you cool your cake layers</strong>, otherwise your frosting will slide right off! I like to cool them in the pans for 15 minutes and then turn the layers onto a cooling rack to cool completely.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 class=\"wp-block-heading\">My Favorite Cream Cheese Frosting</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>This cream cheese frosting reminds me of softly <a href=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/55823/whipped-cream/\" data-type=\"post\" data-id=\"55823\">whipped cream</a>. <strong>It&#8217;s light, creamy, and swoopy.</strong> I highly recommend it, but if you want a firmer, more American-style cream cheese frosting that you can pipe onto the cake, see the tips section of the recipe for my recommendations.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-full\"><noscript><img decoding=\"async\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\" frosting, you will need <strong>cream cheese, powdered sugar, cornstarch, and heavy cream.</strong> You&#8217;ll beat the cream cheese with the sugar and cornstarch until fluffy and then beat in the cream. Watch our video to see how light, swoopy, and creamy it becomes. We also use this frosting for our <a href=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/12208/chocolate-guinness-cake-recipe/\" data-type=\"post\" data-id=\"12208\">Guinness chocolate cake</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure without frosting. You can try it plain or sift some powdered sugar on top. We prefer to use a hand grater when preparing the carrots since it creates delicate shreds that melt into the cake batter. We like using granulated and brown sugar in this recipe. If you only want to use one, choose brown sugar since it has the necessary acid to react with the baking soda.</p>\n<p>Frosting: Our creamy frosting recipe shared below is not a traditional cream cheese frosting. Thanks to whipped cream, it&#8217;s creamier and has soft peaks (you can see it in our video). See the tips section below for a more traditional frosting.</p>\n</div>\n        <div class=\"itr-recipeyield\"><span>Makes 1 (9-inch) double layer cake (16 thin slices) or 22 to 24 cupcakes</span></div>\n        <div class=\"itr-recipe-video\">\n            <h2>Watch Us Make the Recipe</h2>\n            <div class=\"itr-recipe-player\"><iframe loading=\"lazy\" title=\"Easy Moist Carrot Cake Recipe\" width=\"640\" height=\"360\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/imJS5swk0Vc?rel=0\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share\" referrerpolicy=\"strict-origin-when-cross-origin\" allowfullscreen></iframe></div>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"itr-ingredients\">\n            <h2>You Will Need</h2>                \n                    <span class=\"ingredient_heading\">For Carrot Cake</span>                <span class=\"itr-ingredients\"><p>2 cups (260g) all-purpose flour, <em>spooned and leveled</em></p>\n<p>2 teaspoons baking soda, important to level the teaspoon, see tips</p>\n<p>1/2 teaspoon fine sea salt</p>\n<p>1 \u00bd teaspoons ground cinnamon</p>\n<p>1 \u00bc cups (295ml) vegetable oil</p>\n<p>1 cup (200g) granulated sugar</p>\n<p>1 cup (190g) lightly packed brown sugar</p>\n<p>1 teaspoon vanilla extract</p>\n<p>4 large eggs, at room temperature</p>\n<p>3 cups (300g) grated peeled carrots, <em>5 to 6 medium carrots</em></p>\n<p>1 cup (120g) coarsely chopped pecans</p>\n<p>1/2 cup (70g) raisins</p>\n</span>                \n                    <span class=\"ingredient_heading\">For Creamy Frosting</span>                <span class=\"itr-ingredients\"><p>8 ounces (225g) cream cheese, at room temperature</p>\n<p>2 teaspoons cornstarch, optional</p>\n<p>1 \u00bc cups (140g) powdered sugar</p>\n<p>1/3 cup (80ml) cold heavy cream, <em>not plain whipping cream, see tips</em></p>\n<p>1/2 cup (50g) coarsely chopped pecans, for topping cake</p>\n</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"itr-directions\">\n            <h2>Directions</h2>\n                <ul>\n                        <li class=\"itr-step\"><span>Bake Cake</span></li>                    <span class=\"itr-directions\"><p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">1</span>Position a rack in the middle of the oven. Preheat the oven to <strong>350\u00b0F</strong> (176\u00b0C).</p>\n<p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">2</span>Grease two 9-inch round cake pans, line the bottom with parchment paper, and then grease the top. Or grease and flour the bottom and sides of both pans.</p>\n<p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">3</span>Whisk flour, baking soda, salt, and cinnamon in a medium bowl until very well blended.</p>\n<p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">4</span>In a separate bowl, whisk the oil, granulated sugar, brown sugar, and vanilla.</p>\n<p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">5</span>Add the eggs, one at a time, whisking after each one.</p>\n<p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">6</span>Switch to a large rubber spatula. Scrape the sides and bottom of the bowl, then add the dry ingredients in three parts, gently stirring until they disappear and the batter is smooth.</p>\n<p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">7</span>Stir in the carrots, nuts, and raisins.</p>\n<p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">8</span>Divide the cake batter between the prepared cake pans. Bake until the tops of the cake layers are springy when touched and when a toothpick inserted into the center of the cake comes out clean, 35 to 45 minutes.</p>\n<p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">9</span>Cool the cakes in the pans for 15 minutes, then carefully turn the cake layers out onto cooling racks. Remove the parchment paper and cool completely. If you find that a cake layer is sticking to the bottom of the pan, leave the cake pan upside down and allow gravity to do its thing.</p>\n</p>\n                    </span>\n\n                </ul>\n                <ul>\n                        <li class=\"itr-step\"><span>Frost Cake</span></li>                    <span class=\"itr-directions\"><p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">1</span>In a large bowl, beat the cream cheese with a handheld mixer on medium speed until smooth and creamy, about 1 minute.</p>\n<p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">2</span>Beat in the powdered sugar and cornstarch. I like sifting the powdered sugar and cornstarch over the cream cheese to remove lumps. If you do not have a fine mesh sieve, beat in the cornstarch and powdered sugar a 1/4 cup at a time until combined.</p>\n<p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">3</span>Pour in the heavy cream. Beat on medium speed for 2 to 3 minutes or until the frosting is whipped and creamy. This frosting resembles the texture of whipped cream. Chill covered until ready to frost the cake.</p>\n<p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">4</span>When the cake layers are completely cool, frost the top of one cake layer and place the second cake layer on top.</p>\n<p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">5</span>Add the remaining frosting to the top of the carrot cake and use a butter knife or small spatula to swirl the frosting around. Leave the sides of the cake unfrosted. Finish with a handful of nuts on top.</p>\n</p>\n                    </span>\n\n                </ul>\n                <ul>\n                        <li class=\"itr-step\"><span>Storing</span></li>                    <span class=\"itr-directions\"><p><span class=\"itr-step-num\">1</span>Frosted carrot cake lasts in the refrigerator for up to 1 week. I keep it covered with plastic wrap or use a cake keeper, or large bowl turned upside down to cover the cake. I do not recommend freezing frosted carrot cake (the frosting does not thaw well). You can refrigerate unfrosted cake layers for up 5 days or freeze them for up to 3 months. Thaw overnight in the fridge before adding your frosting.</p>\n</p>\n                    </span>\n\n                </ul>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"itr-notes\">\n            <h2>Adam and Joanne's Tips</h2>\n            <div class=\"tip\"><ul>\n<li><strong>Measuring the flour:</strong> Either weigh it or use the \u201cspoon and level\u201d method: Fluff the flour, spoon it into the measuring cup, then level off the top with a flat edge. See our video for a demonstration.</li>\n<li><strong>Baking soda:</strong> When measuring, dip your spoon into the container, then level it off using the straight edge of one of your other spoons. For the best results, use fresh baking soda (it loses its potency after being opened for 6 months).</li>\n<li><strong>Traditional cream cheese frosting:</strong> In a large bowl, beat 16 ounces of cream cheese and 1/2 cup of softened butter together for a minute or two until smooth. Add 4 \u00bd cups of powdered sugar, 1 \u00bc teaspoons of vanilla extract, and a pinch of salt. Beat for 2 to 3 minutes until extra creamy. If it is too thick, add 1 tablespoon of cream or milk.</li>\n<li><strong>How to make carrot cake cupcakes:</strong> This recipe makes 24 cupcakes. Bake them for 14 to 18 minutes and allow to cool in the cupcake pan before cooling completely on a wire rack. You may also like this recipe for <a href=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/46269/carrot-cake-cupcakes/\">carrot cake cupcakes</a>.</li>\n<li><strong>To make a large single-layer cake</strong>, add all the batter to a 9 x 13-inch rectangular pan and bake. The bake time may be slightly longer. A 10-cup or 12-cup bundt pan should also work, but expect the bake time to increase by 30%.</li>\n<li><strong>Adding pineapple:</strong> I like fresh chopped pineapple or drained canned pineapple. Do not add more than 1 cup.</li>\n<li><strong>Heavy cream (US bakers):</strong> Heavy cream has more milk fat (about 36%), while whipping cream has less (around 30%). Use &#8220;heavy cream&#8221; or &#8220;heavy whipping cream.&#8221; Plain &#8220;whipping cream&#8221; does not whip as well and can cause your frosting to be too soft. If you only have whipping cream or cream with less than 35% fat content: If you only have whipping cream or are unsure what you have in your kitchen, whisk it in a separate bowl until soft peaks. Add a couple of spoonfuls of the whipped cream to the beaten cream cheese mixture and combine to loosen. Then, fold in the remaining whipped cream.</li>\n<li><strong>UK &amp; Australia bakers:</strong> Use plain flour for the batter and &#8220;double cream&#8221; or &#8220;thickened cream&#8221; with at least 35% fat content for the creamy frosting.</li>\n<li>Recipe inspired by Smitten Kitchen&#8217;s cupcakes recipe.</li>\n<li>The nutrition facts provided below are estimates.</li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <div class=\"itr-nutrition\">\n            <span class=\"nutrition-heading\">Nutrition Per Serving</span><span>\n                <span>Serving Size</span>\n class=\"related-recipe\">\n                        <div class=\"related-image\">\n                            <a href=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/50401/aquafaba/\" title=\"How to Make Aquafaba (Ultimate Guide)\">\n                                <noscript><img decoding=\"async\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\" src=\"https://www.inspiredtaste.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Aquafaba-1200.jpg\" 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></noscript><img decoding=\"async\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\"
